float _determinant2(mat2 m) {
return m[0].x*m[1].y - m[0].y*m[1].x;
float _determinant3(mat3 m) {
 a00 = m[0].x, a01 = m[0].y, a02 = m[0].z,
 a10 = m[1].x, a11 = m[1].y, a12 = m[1].z,
 a20 = m[2].x, a21 = m[2].y, a22 = m[2].z,
 b01 = a22*a11 - a12*a21,
 b11 =-a22*a10 + a12*a20,
 b21 = a21*a10 - a11*a20;
return a00*b01 + a01*b11 + a02*b21;
mat4 _determinant4(mat4 m) {
 a00 = m[0].x, a01 = m[0].y, a02 = m[0].z, a03 = m[0].w,
 a10 = m[1].x, a11 = m[1].y, a12 = m[1].z, a13 = m[1].w,
 a20 = m[2].x, a21 = m[2].y, a22 = m[2].z, a23 = m[2].w,
 a30 = m[3].x, a31 = m[3].y, a32 = m[3].z, a33 = m[3].w,
 b00 = a00*a11 - a01*a10,
 b01 = a00*a12 - a02*a10,
 b02 = a00*a13 - a03*a10,
 b03 = a01*a12 - a02*a11,
 b04 = a01*a13 - a03*a11,
 b05 = a02*a13 - a03*a12,
 b06 = a20*a31 - a21*a30,
 b07 = a20*a32 - a22*a30,
 b08 = a20*a33 - a23*a30,
 b09 = a21*a32 - a22*a31,
 b10 = a21*a33 - a23*a31,
 b11 = a22*a33 - a23*a32;
return b00*b11 - b01*b10 + b02*b09 + b03*b08 - b04*b07 + b05*b06;
mat2 _inverse2(mat2 m) {
return mat2(m[1].y, -m[0].y, -m[1].x, m[0].x) / (m[0].x * m[1].y - m[0].y * m[1].x);
mat3 _inverse3(mat3 m) {
 a00 = m[0].x, a01 = m[0].y, a02 = m[0].z,
 a10 = m[1].x, a11 = m[1].y, a12 = m[1].z,
 a20 = m[2].x, a21 = m[2].y, a22 = m[2].z,
 b01 = a22*a11 - a12*a21,
 b11 =-a22*a10 + a12*a20,
 b21 = a21*a10 - a11*a20,
 det = a00*b01 + a01*b11 + a02*b21;
return mat3(
 b01, (-a22*a01 + a02*a21), ( a12*a01 - a02*a11),
 b11, ( a22*a00 - a02*a20), (-a12*a00 + a02*a10),
 b21, (-a21*a00 + a01*a20), ( a11*a00 - a01*a10)) / det;
mat4 _inverse4(mat4 m) {
 a00 = m[0].x, a01 = m[0].y, a02 = m[0].z, a03 = m[0].w,
 a10 = m[1].x, a11 = m[1].y, a12 = m[1].z, a13 = m[1].w,
 a20 = m[2].x, a21 = m[2].y, a22 = m[2].z, a23 = m[2].w,
 a30 = m[3].x, a31 = m[3].y, a32 = m[3].z, a33 = m[3].w,
 b00 = a00*a11 - a01*a10,
 b01 = a00*a12 - a02*a10,
 b02 = a00*a13 - a03*a10,
 b03 = a01*a12 - a02*a11,
 b04 = a01*a13 - a03*a11,
 b05 = a02*a13 - a03*a12,
 b06 = a20*a31 - a21*a30,
 b07 = a20*a32 - a22*a30,
 b08 = a20*a33 - a23*a30,
 b09 = a21*a32 - a22*a31,
 b10 = a21*a33 - a23*a31,
 b11 = a22*a33 - a23*a32,
 det = b00*b11 - b01*b10 + b02*b09 + b03*b08 - b04*b07 + b05*b06;
return mat4(
 a11*b11 - a12*b10 + a13*b09,
 a02*b10 - a01*b11 - a03*b09,
 a31*b05 - a32*b04 + a33*b03,
 a22*b04 - a21*b05 - a23*b03,
 a12*b08 - a10*b11 - a13*b07,
 a00*b11 - a02*b08 + a03*b07,
 a32*b02 - a30*b05 - a33*b01,
 a20*b05 - a22*b02 + a23*b01,
 a10*b10 - a11*b08 + a13*b06,
 a01*b08 - a00*b10 - a03*b06,
 a30*b04 - a31*b02 + a33*b00,
 a21*b02 - a20*b04 - a23*b00,
 a11*b07 - a10*b09 - a12*b06,
 a00*b09 - a01*b07 + a02*b06,
 a31*b01 - a30*b03 - a32*b00,
 a20*b03 - a21*b01 + a22*b00) / det;
